Financial Evolution: AI, Machine Learning and Sentiment Analysis

Wed, 4 November –≤ 12:00, —Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è.

The event will discover the applications of AI & ML in the financial services industry. The opportunities of sharing knowledge and exploiting IP in the finance domain are also going to be discussed. Additionally, it is a great chance for professionals from finance industry to interact and communicate with each other via this online mode of conference. Here are some of the things you can look forward to in the event: Learn how you can benefit from the unprecedented progress in technological advances for yourself and your company Find out about the impact of Alternative Data from multiple sources Benefit from the experience of world class presenters from UK, US and India Gain exclusive insights into pioneering projects in AI, Machine Learning & Sentiment Analysis in Finance Programme includes the latest state-of-the-art research, practical applications and case studies Enjoy excellent networking opportunities throughout the days with all participants, including presenters, investors and exhibitors
